**Based on work by Martín Escardó.**

Preliminaries
=============

We assume a fixed frame `F` on which to define the frame of nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="729" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="736" href="FrameOfNuclei.html" class="Module">FrameOfNuclei</a> <a id="750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="751" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="755" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="761" href="Basis.html#3042" class="Generalizable">𝒰</a> <a id="763" href="Basis.html#3044" class="Generalizable">𝒱</a> <a id="765" href="Basis.html#3046" class="Generalizable">𝒲</a><a id="766" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="768" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="787" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="792" href="Poset.html#3652" class="Module">PosetReasoning</a> <a id="807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="808" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="812" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="813" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="815" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="822" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">_⊑⟨_⟩_</a><a id="828" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="830" href="Poset.html#3832" class="Function Operator">_■</a><a id="832" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
For simplicity, we will refer to the order, the meet, and the join of `F` simply
as `⊑`, _⊓_`, and `⋁_`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊑_"></a><a id="953" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#953" class="Function Operator">_⊑_</a> <a id="957" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="959" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="961" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="963" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="968" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="970" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="972" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="975" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="977" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="983" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a>
<a id="985" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#985" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="987" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#953" class="Function Operator">⊑</a> <a id="989" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#989" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="991" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="993" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#985" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="995" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="998" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1002" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1004" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1006" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#989" class="Bound">y</a>

<a id="_⊓_"></a><a id="1009" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">_⊓_</a> <a id="1013" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1015" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1017" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1019" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1022" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1024" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1026" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1028" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1031" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1033" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1035" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1037" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="1040" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1040" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1042" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="1044" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1044" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="1046" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1048" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1040" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1050" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">⊓[</a> <a id="1053" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1055" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1057" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1044" class="Bound">y</a>

<a id="⋁_"></a><a id="1060" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁_</a> <a id="1063" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1065" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="1069" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1071" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1073" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1075" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1078" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1080" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1082" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1084" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="1087" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="1089" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1089" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1091" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1093" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="1096" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1098" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="1100" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1089" class="Bound">U</a>
</pre>
We define the notion of Scott-continuity of a nucleus on `F` as follows:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="isScottCont′"></a><a id="1189" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1189" class="Function">isScottCont′</a> <a id="1202" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1204" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1205" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1207" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1209" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1212" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1214" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1216" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1218" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1220" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1224" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1225" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="1227" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1229" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="1231" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1233" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1235" href="Basis.html#3138" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="1236" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1238" href="Basis.html#3184" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="1240" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1189" class="Function">isScottCont′</a> <a id="1253" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1253" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1255" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1259" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1260" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1260" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1262" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1264" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="1268" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1270" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1272" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1274" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1276" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1278" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="1284" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="1286" href="Poset.html#7416" class="Function">isDirected</a> <a id="1297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1298" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1302" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1303" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1305" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1260" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1307" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="1309" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1311" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1253" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1314" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="1316" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1260" class="Bound">U</a><a id="1317" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1319" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="1321" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="1324" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1326" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="1328" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="1330" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1253" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1332" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1336" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1334" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="1336" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1336" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1338" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="1340" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1260" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1342" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a>

<a id="isScottCont"></a><a id="1345" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1359" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1367" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1369" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1371" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1372" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="1374" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1376" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="1378" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1380" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1382" href="Basis.html#3138" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="1383" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1385" href="Basis.html#3184" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="1387" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1399" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1400" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1400" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1402" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1404" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="1407" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1409" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1189" class="Function">isScottCont′</a> <a id="1422" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1400" class="Bound">j</a>
</pre>
The type expression the notion of being Scott-continuous is an h-proposition
as one would expect:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="isScottCont-prop"></a><a id="1536" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1536" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a> <a id="1553" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1556" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1556" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="1558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1560" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1568" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1571" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1573" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10148" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="1580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1581" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1593" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1556" class="Bound">𝒿</a><a id="1594" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1596" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1536" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a> <a id="1613" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1613" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1615" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1619" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#14996" class="Function">isPropΠ</a> <a id="1627" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="1629" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1629" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1633" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#14996" class="Function">isPropΠ</a> <a id="1641" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="1643" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1643" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="1645" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1647" href="Poset.html#3444" class="Function">carrier-is-set</a> <a id="1662" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1663" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1667" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1668" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1670" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="1672" class="Symbol">_</a>
</pre>
We define a shorthand for the type of Scott-continuous nuclei as we will be
primarily interested in those:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ScottContNucleus"></a><a id="1795" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="1812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1815" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="1817" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1819" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="1821" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1823" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1825" href="Basis.html#3138" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="1826" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1828" href="Basis.html#3184" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="1830" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="1847" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1849" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="1852" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1852" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1854" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="1856" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1864" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1866" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1868" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1880" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1852" class="Bound">j</a>

<a id="ScottContNucleus-set"></a><a id="1883" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1883" class="Function">ScottContNucleus-set</a> <a id="1904" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1906" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10203" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="1912" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a>
<a id="1929" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1883" class="Function">ScottContNucleus-set</a> <a id="1950" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1954" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#12444" class="Function">isSetΣ</a> <a id="1961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1962" href="Nucleus.html#1482" class="Function">Nucleus-set</a> <a id="1974" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1975" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1978" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#13767" class="Function">isProp→isSet</a> <a id="1991" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="1993" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1536" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a><a id="2009" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Poset of nuclei on `F` (`𝔑`)
============================

The set of endofunctions on a given frame forms a poset under the pointwise
order; we denote by `_⊑f_` this pointwise order and by `𝔉` this poset.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊑f_"></a><a id="2231" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2231" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="2236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2238" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2239" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2241" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2243" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2246" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2248" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2250" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2252" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="2254" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2256" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2258" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2259" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2261" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2263" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2266" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2268" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2270" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2272" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="2274" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2276" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2278" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="2284" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2285" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="2287" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="2289" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="2290" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2292" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2292" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2294" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2231" class="Function Operator">⊑f</a> <a id="2297" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2297" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2299" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2301" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">∀[</a> <a id="2304" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2304" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2306" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">∶</a> <a id="2308" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2310" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2312" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2315" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2317" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2292" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2319" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2304" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2321" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="2324" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="2328" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2330" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2332" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2297" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2334" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2304" class="Bound">x</a>

</pre>
We denote by `𝔑` the poset of nuclei:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝔑"></a><a id="2948" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="2950" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2952" href="Poset.html#2165" class="Function">Poset</a> <a id="2958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2959" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="2961" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="2963" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="2964" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2967" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="2969" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="2971" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="2972" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="3008" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="3016" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3016" class="Function">𝔑-str</a> <a id="3022" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3024" href="Poset.html#1701" class="Function">PosetStr</a> <a id="3033" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3034" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="3036" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="3038" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="3039" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3041" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3042" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="3050" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="3051" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="3055" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3016" class="Function">𝔑-str</a> <a id="3061" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3063" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3136" class="Function Operator">_⊑n_</a> <a id="3068" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3070" href="Nucleus.html#1482" class="Function">Nucleus-set</a> <a id="3082" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3084" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3086" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2337" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="3094" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="3096" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="3100" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3102" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3206" class="Function">⊑-trans</a> <a id="3110" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3112" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3312" class="Function">⊑-antisym</a>
    <a id="3126" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="3136" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3136" class="Function Operator">_⊑n_</a> <a id="3141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3143" href="Poset.html#275" class="Function">Order</a> <a id="3149" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3150" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="3152" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="3154" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#763" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="3155" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3157" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3158" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="3166" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="3167" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="3173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3174" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3174" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="3176" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3178" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="3181" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3136" class="Function Operator">⊑n</a> <a id="3184" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3185" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3185" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3187" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3189" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="3192" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3194" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3174" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="3196" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2231" class="Function Operator">⊑f</a> <a id="3199" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3185" class="Bound">k</a>

    <a id="3206" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3206" class="Function">⊑-trans</a> <a id="3214" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3216" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="3218" href="Poset.html#622" class="Function">isTransitive</a> <a id="3231" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3136" class="Function Operator">_⊑n_</a> <a id="3236" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>

    <a id="6544" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6544" class="Function">⦅𝟒⦆</a> <a id="6548" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6550" href="Frame.html#15060" class="Function">cleft</a>  <a id="6557" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6559" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6561" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6562" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="6565" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6567" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">]-lower₀</a> <a id="6576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6577" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5132" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6580" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5132" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6582" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6583" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6586" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6587" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5132" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6590" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5162" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6592" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6593" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="6601" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6601" class="Function">⦅𝟓⦆</a> <a id="6605" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6607" href="Frame.html#15060" class="Function">cleft</a>  <a id="6614" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6616" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6619" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5150" class="Bound">j-n₂</a> <a id="6624" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6625" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6631" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6631" class="Function">⦅𝟔⦆</a> <a id="6635" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6637" href="Frame.html#14702" class="Function">cright</a> <a id="6644" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6646" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6649" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5180" class="Bound">k-n₂</a> <a id="6654" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6655" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We now prove that `_⊓n_` is a greatest lower bound operator as expected:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊓n-meet"></a><a id="6744" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6744" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="6752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6754" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="6756" href="Frame.html#1300" class="Function">isGLB</a> <a id="6762" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="6764" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">_⊓n_</a> <a id="6769" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="6771" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6744" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="6779" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6781" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6805" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="6784" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6786" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6972" class="Function">greatest</a>
  <a id="6797" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="6805" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6805" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="6808" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6810" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6811" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6811" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6813" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6813" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6815" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6817" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="6825" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="6826" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6828" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6830" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="6832" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6833" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6811" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6835" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="6838" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6813" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6839" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6841" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="6844" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="6846" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="6848" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6811" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6850" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#538" class="Function Operator">∧</a> <a id="6852" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6853" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6811" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6855" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="6858" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6813" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6859" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6861" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="6864" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="6866" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="6868" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6813" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6870" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
  <a id="6874" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6805" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="6877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6878" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6878" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6880" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6882" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="6885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6886" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6888" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6890" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="6893" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6899" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="6902" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6902" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6904" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6906" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="6909" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6911" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">]-lower₀</a> <a id="6920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6921" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6878" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6923" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6902" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6924" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6927" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6929" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6902" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6930" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6933" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6935" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="6938" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6938" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6940" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6942" href="Frame.html#5023" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="6945" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6947" href="Frame.html#5023" class="Function Operator">]-lower₁</a> <a id="6956" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6957" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6878" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6959" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6938" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6960" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6962" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6963" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6965" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6938" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6966" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="6972" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6972" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="6981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6983" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6984" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6984" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6986" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6986" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6988" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6988" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6992" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7000" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7001" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="7014" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7016" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="7018" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6988" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7020" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7023" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7025" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7027" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6984" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7029" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#538" class="Function Operator">∧</a> <a id="7031" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6988" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7033" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7036" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7038" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7040" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6986" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7042" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#1956" class="Function Operator">⇒</a> <a id="7044" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6988" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7046" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7049" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7051" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7053" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7054" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6984" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7056" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="7059" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6986" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7060" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7062" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
  <a id="7066" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6972" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="7075" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7076" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7076" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7078" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7080" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7083" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7084" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7084" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7086" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7088" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7091" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7092" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7092" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7094" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7096" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7100" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7100" class="Bound">l⊑j</a> <a id="7104" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7106" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7106" class="Bound">l⊑k</a><a id="7109" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7111" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7113" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="7119" href="Frame.html#5153" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="7122" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="7124" href="Frame.html#5153" class="Function Operator">]-greatest</a> <a id="7135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7136" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7076" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7138" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7139" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7141" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7142" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7084" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7144" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7145" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7148" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7092" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7150" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7151" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7153" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7154" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7100" class="Bound">l⊑j</a> <a id="7158" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7159" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7161" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7162" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7106" class="Bound">l⊑k</a> <a id="7166" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7167" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
The meet of two Scott-continuous nuclei is itself Scott-continuous:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊓n-sc"></a><a id="7251" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7251" class="Function">⊓n-sc</a> <a id="7257" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7259" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7260" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7260" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="7262" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7262" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="7264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7266" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7274" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7275" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7277" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7279" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7291" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7260" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="7293" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7295" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7307" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7262" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="7309" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7311" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7324" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7260" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="7326" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="7329" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7262" class="Bound">𝓀</a><a id="7330" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7332" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7251" class="Function">⊓n-sc</a> <a id="7338" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7338" class="Bound">𝒿</a><a id="7339" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="7341" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7341" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7343" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7345" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7348" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7348" class="Bound">𝓀</a><a id="7349" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="7351" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7351" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7353" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7355" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7358" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7358" class="Bound">j-sc</a> <a id="7363" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7363" class="Bound">k-sc</a> <a id="7368" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="7370" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7370" class="Bound">U-dir</a><a id="7375" class="Symbol">@(_</a> <a id="7379" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7381" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7381" class="Bound">U-up</a><a id="7385" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7387" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="7391" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7341" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7394" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7396" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a><a id="7397" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7399" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="7401" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7351" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7403" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7404" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7406" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a><a id="7407" class="Symbol">)</a>                                             <a id="7453" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="7456" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8302" class="Function">⦅𝟏⦆</a> <a id="7460" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
  <a id="7464" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7465" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7467" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="7469" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7341" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7471" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7475" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7473" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="7475" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7475" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7477" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="7479" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="7481" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a><a id="7482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7484" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="7486" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7351" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7489" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7491" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a><a id="7492" class="Symbol">)</a>                                 <a id="7526" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="7529" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8345" class="Function">⦅𝟐⦆</a> <a id="7533" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
  <a id="7537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7538" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7540" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="7542" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7341" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7544" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7548" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7546" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="7548" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7548" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7550" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="7552" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="7554" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a><a id="7555" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7557" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="7559" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7560" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7562" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="7564" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7351" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7566" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7570" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7568" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="7570" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7570" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7572" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="7574" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="7576" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a><a id="7577" class="Symbol">)</a>                     <a id="7599" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="7602" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8388" class="Function">⦅𝟑⦆</a> <a id="7606" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
  <a id="7610" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1060" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7613" href="Basis.html#6348" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="7615"   <a id="8388" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8388" class="Function">⦅𝟑⦆</a>  <a id="8393" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8395" href="Frame.html#13246" class="Function">sym-distr</a> <a id="8405" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="8407" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="8409" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7341" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="8411" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8415" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8413" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="8415" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8415" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8417" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="8419" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="8421" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a> <a id="8423" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="8425" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7351" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8427" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8431" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8429" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="8431" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8431" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8433" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="8435" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7368" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="8437" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a>
  <a id="8441" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8441" class="Function">⦅𝟒⦆</a>  <a id="8446" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8448" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="8451" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="8455" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="8457" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">]-antisym</a> <a id="8467" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8469" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8471" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8193" class="Function">⦅𝟒a⦆</a> <a id="8476" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8224" class="Function">⦅𝟒b⦆</a>
</pre>
Using all these, we define the meet of two Scott-continuous nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊓sc_"></a><a id="8563" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8563" class="Function Operator">_⊓sc_</a> <a id="8569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8571" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="8588" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8590" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="8607" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8609" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a>
<a id="8626" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8563" class="Function Operator">_⊓sc_</a> <a id="8632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8633" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8633" class="Bound">𝒿</a><a id="8634" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="8636" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8636" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="8638" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8640" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8643" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8645" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8645" class="Bound">j-sc</a><a id="8649" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8651" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8652" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8652" class="Bound">𝓀</a><a id="8653" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="8655" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8655" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8657" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8659" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8662" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8664" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8664" class="Bound">k-sc</a><a id="8668" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8670" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8672" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8633" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8674" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="8677" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8652" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8679" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8681" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7251" class="Function">⊓n-sc</a> <a id="8687" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8633" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8689" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8652" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8691" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8645" class="Bound">j-sc</a> <a id="8696" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8664" class="Bound">k-sc</a>
</pre>
which we verify to be a GLB operator as expected:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊓sc-meet"></a><a id="8765" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8765" class="Function">⊓sc-meet</a> <a id="8774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8776" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8778" href="Frame.html#1300" class="Function">isGLB</a> <a id="8784" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3637" class="Function">𝔖</a> <a id="8786" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8563" class="Function Operator">_⊓sc_</a> <a id="8792" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="8794" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="8798" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8765" class="Function">⊓sc-meet</a> <a id="8807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8808" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8808" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8810" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8812" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8815" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8816" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8816" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8818" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8820" class="Symbol">_)</a>          <a id="8832" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8834" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="8838" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6744" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="8846" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8808" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8848" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8816" class="Bound">𝓀</a>
<a id="8850" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#560" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="8854" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8765" class="Function">⊓sc-meet</a> <a id="8863" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8864" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8864" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8866" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8868" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8871" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8872" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8872" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8874" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8876" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8879" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8880" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8880" class="Bound">𝓀′</a> <a id="8883" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8885" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8888" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8890" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#560" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="8894" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6744" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="8902" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8864" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8904" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8872" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8906" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8880" class="Bound">𝓀′</a>
</pre>
Arbitrary join of nuclei
------------------------

This is the non-trivial part of this development.

### Directification of a family of nuclei

We first define following function `ℜ` such that, given a family `U ≔ { fᵢ : A →
A ∣ i ∈ I }` of endofunctions, and a list `i₀, …, iₙ` of indices from `I`, `ℜ U
[i₀, …, iₙ]` denotes the composition `fᵢₙ ∘ ⋯ ∘ fᵢ₀`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℜ"></a><a id="9283" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9287" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9288" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9290" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9292" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9297" href="Basis.html#2593" class="Generalizable">ℓ</a><a id="9298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9300" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9303" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9303" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9305" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9307" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9311" href="Basis.html#2595" class="Generalizable">ℓ′</a> <a id="9314" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9315" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9317" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9319" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9320" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9323" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9325" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="9330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9331" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="9337" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9303" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9338" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9340" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9342" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9344" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9346" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="9348" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9350" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9350" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9352" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#185" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>       <a id="9361" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9363" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="9369" class="Symbol">_</a>
<a id="9371" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9373" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9373" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9375" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9376" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9376" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9378" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="9380" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9380" class="Bound">is</a><a id="9382" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9384" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9386" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9388" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9373" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9390" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9380" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="9393" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="9395" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9396" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9373" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9398" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="9400" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9376" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9401" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Using `ℜ`, we define the family obtained from such a family of endofunctions
that consists of all such compositions.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℜ-fam"></a><a id="9534" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="9540" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9542" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9543" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9547" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9552" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">𝒰</a><a id="9553" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9556" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9556" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9560" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9564" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="9566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9567" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9569" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9571" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9572" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9575" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9577" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9581" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="9583" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9584" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9588" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9589" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9591" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="9597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9598" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="9600" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9602" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9602" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9603" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9605" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9605" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9607" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9609" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="9614" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9615" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="9621" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9605" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9622" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9624" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9626" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9628" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9605" class="Bound">α</a>
</pre>
We will use this function to compute the join of a family of nuclei. The key
idea is that the family of compositions is a directed family even if the family
we start with is not.

Notice that the identity function is always a (pre)nucleus.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="id-is-nuclear"></a><a id="9884" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9884" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="9898" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9901" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9901" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9905" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="9911" href="Basis.html#2598" class="Generalizable">ℓ₀</a> <a id="9914" href="Basis.html#2601" class="Generalizable">ℓ₁</a> <a id="9917" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a><a id="9918" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9920" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9922" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="9935" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9901" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9938" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="9944" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9946" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9901" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9948" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="9950" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9952" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9884" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="9966" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9966" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9968" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9970" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9973" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9973" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="9975" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9975" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="9977" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9979" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="9983" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9985" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9987" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="9990" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="9994" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9966" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9996" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a>
</pre>
Compositions of prenuclei are prenuclei meaning given a family of nuclei, its
`ℜ-fam` is a family of prenuclei

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℜ-fam-prenucleus"></a><a id="10128" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10128" class="Function">ℜ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10148" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10148" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10150" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10152" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="10156" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="10158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10159" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10161" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10163" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="10166" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10168" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10170" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10172" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="10174" class="Symbol">))</a>
                 <a id="10194" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10196" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10198" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10198" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="10200" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10202" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="10208" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10148" class="Bound">K</a><a id="10209" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10211" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10213" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10226" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10228" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10229" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10148" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10231" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="10233" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10198" class="Bound">i</a><a id="10234" class="Symbol">))</a>
                 <a id="10254" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10257" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10257" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="10260" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10262" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="10267" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10268" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="10274" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10148" class="Bound">K</a><a id="10275" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10280" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10293" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10295" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10296" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="10302" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10148" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10304" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="10306" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10257" class="Bound">is</a><a id="10308" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10310" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10128" class="Function">ℜ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10327" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10329" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10331" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#185" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>       <a id="10340" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10342" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9884" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="10356" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a>
<a id="10358" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10128" class="Function">ℜ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10375" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10375" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10377" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10377" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="10379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10380" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10380" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="10382" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="10384" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10384" class="Bound">is</a><a id="10386" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10388" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10390" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10661" class="Function">n₀</a> <a id="10393" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10395" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11002" class="Function">n₁</a>
  <a id="10400" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="10408" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10408" class="Function">j</a> <a id="10410" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10412" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="10418" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10375" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10420" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="10422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10423" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10380" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="10425" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="10427" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10384" class="Bound">is</a><a id="10429" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="10434" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10434" class="Function">j′</a> <a id="10437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10439" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10441" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10443" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="10446" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10448" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10450" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10452" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
  <a id="10457" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10434" class="Function">j′</a> <a id="10460" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10462" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="10468" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10375" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10470" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="10472" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10384" class="Bound">is</a>

  <a id="10478" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10478" class="Function">ih</a> <a id="10481" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10483" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10496" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10498" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10434" class="Function">j′</a>

</pre>
For convenience, we introduce the following notation: given a some family
`J` of nuclei, `J ^*` denotes its `ℜ-fam`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_^*"></a><a id="11242" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11242" class="Function Operator">_^*</a> <a id="11246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11248" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="11252" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="11254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11255" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="11263" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="11264" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11266" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11268" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="11272" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="11274" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11275" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="11277" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="11279" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="11282" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11284" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="11286" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="11288" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="11290" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="11292" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11292" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="11294" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11242" class="Function Operator">^*</a> <a id="11297" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11299" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="11305" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="11307" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11312" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="11309" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="11311" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11311" class="Bound">(</a><a id="11312" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11312" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="11314" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11316" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11311" class="Bound">_)</a> <a id="11319" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="11321" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11292" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="11323" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a>

`J ^*` is always inhabited.

</pre>
Some nice notation for applying a certain nucleus in a family to an argument.

</pre>
`J^*` is upwards-closed.

  <a id="13467" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13442" class="Function">Jᵢₛ₊₊ⱼₛ</a> <a id="13475" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13477" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12919" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13479" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12352" class="Function Operator">*⦅</a> <a id="13482" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12921" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="13485" href="Cubical.Data.List.Base.html#335" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="13488" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12924" class="Bound">js</a> <a id="13491" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12352" class="Function Operator">⦆_</a> <a id="13494" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13496" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13187" class="Function">J*-prenuclear</a> <a id="13510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13511" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12921" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="13514" href="Cubical.Data.List.Base.html#335" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="13517" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12924" class="Bound">js</a><a id="13519" class="Symbol">)</a>

<pre class="Agda"><a id="J*-directed"></a><a id="13530" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13530" class="Function">J*-directed</a> <a id="13542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13544" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13545" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13545" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13547" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13549" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="13553" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="13555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13556" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="13564" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="13565" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13568" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13570" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="13572" href="Poset.html#7416" class="Function">isDirected</a> <a id="13583" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2708" class="Function">𝔉</a> <a id="13585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13586" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13545" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13588" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11242" class="Function Operator">^*</a><a id="13590" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13592" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="13594" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13530" class="Function">J*-directed</a> <a id="13606" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13606" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13608" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13610" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12091" class="Function">J*-inhabited</a> <a id="13623" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13606" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13625" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13627" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13629" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13629" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="13632" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13632" class="Bound">js</a> <a id="13635" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13637" href="Basis.html#7744" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∣</a> <a id="13639" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12762" class="Function">J*-up</a> <a id="13645" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13606" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13647" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13629" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="13650" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13632" class="Bound">js</a> <a id="13653" href="Basis.html#7744" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∣</a>
</pre>
Given a family `J` of Scott-continuous nuclei, everything in `J ^*` is
Scott-continuous.

  <a id="15539" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15530" class="Function">up</a> <a id="15542" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15544" href="Frame.html#5772" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="15547" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="15549" href="Frame.html#5772" class="Function Operator">]-least</a> <a id="15557" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="15559" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="15561" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15563" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="15565" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15565" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="15567" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15569" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15569" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15571" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15573" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15573" class="Bound">j</a><a id="15574" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15576" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15578" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15578" class="Bound">eq</a><a id="15580" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15582" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15584" href="Frame.html#5336" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="15587" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="15589" href="Frame.html#5336" class="Function Operator">]-upper</a> <a id="15597" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="15599" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15565" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="15601" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15603" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15573" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="15605" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15607" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15569" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15608" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15610" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15612" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15578" class="Bound">eq</a><a id="15614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15616" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="15621" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15621" class="Function">⦅𝟏⦆</a> <a id="15625" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15627" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#955" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="15631" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15632" href="Frame.html#11918" class="Function">flatten</a> <a id="15640" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="15642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15643" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="15649" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15152" class="Bound">U</a><a id="15650" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15652" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15655" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15655" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="15657" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15659" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="15665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15666" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15150" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="15668" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11242" class="Function Operator">^*</a><a id="15670" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15673" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15675" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15675" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15677" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15677" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="15679" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15681" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15150" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="15683" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12352" class="Function Operator">*⦅</a> <a id="15686" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15677" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="15688" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12352" class="Function Operator">⦆</a> <a id="15690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15691" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15152" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="15693" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="15695" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15675" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15696" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="15701" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15701" class="Function">⦅𝟐⦆</a> <a id="15705" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15707" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="15710" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="15714" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="15716" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">]-antisym</a> <a id="15726" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="15728" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="15730" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15435" class="Function">down</a> <a id="15735" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#15530" class="Function">up</a>

</pre>
Some shorthand notation that we will use when defining the join.

### The definition of the join

Distributivity
--------------

We construct a rather involved proof of the fact that binary meets distribute
over arbitrary joins.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="dupl"></a><a id="21270" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21270" class="Function">dupl</a> <a id="21275" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21278" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21278" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21280" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21280" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21282" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21284" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="21286" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21288" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="21290" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21292" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21294" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="21296" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21278" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21298" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21300" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21280" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21302" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="21305" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="21309" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21311" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="21313" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21278" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21315" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21317" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21318" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21278" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21320" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21322" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21280" class="Bound">y</a><a id="21323" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21325" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
